REQUEST AUTHENTICATORS - These process HTTP requests directly:\\n   - The request union authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/union/union.go) chains multiple request authenticators\\n   - Front-proxy/header-based authenticator (headerrequest) for front proxy scenarios\\n   - Client certificate (x509) authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/x509/x509.go) - verifies client certificates and extracts user info from CommonName and Organization\\n   - Bearer token authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/bearertoken/bearertoken.go) - extracts bearer tokens from Authorization header\\n   - WebSocket protocol authenticator for WebSocket upgrades\\n   - Anonymous authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/anonymous/anonymous.go) - allows unauthenticated access as system:anonymous user\\n\\n2. TOKEN AUTHENTICATORS - These verify extracted bearer tokens:\\n   - Token file authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/token/tokenfile/tokenfile.go) - verifies tokens from a CSV file\\n   - Service account JWT authenticator (pkg/serviceaccount/jwt.go) - verifies Kubernetes service account tokens using JWT validation\\n   - Bootstrap token authenticator (plugin/pkg/auth/authenticator/token/bootstrap/bootstrap.go) - handles cluster bootstrap tokens from kube-system namespace\\n   - Webhook token authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/authenticator/token/webhook/webhook.go) - delegates token verification to a webhook server\\n   - Token caching authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/token/cache/cache.go) - caches authentication results\\n\\nThe complete chain construction flow in Config.New() is:\\n1. Request authenticators are added first: front-proxy header authenticator, then client certificates\\n2. Token authenticators are combined into a union via tokenunion.New()\\n3. The token union is wrapped with caching if configured\\n4. Bearer token request authenticator wraps the token union to extract and verify bearer tokens\\n5. The request authenticators union (union.New()) combines all request authenticators\\n6. AuthenticatedGroupAdder wraps the chain to add system:authenticated group to successful authentications\\n7. Finally, the anonymous authenticator is added as a fallback using NewFailOnError() to handle unauthenticated requests\\n\\nThe delegating authenticator factory (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/authenticatorfactory/delegating.go) provides a similar but simpler chain for non-API-server components that need to verify tokens against the API server.\\n\\nKey architectural decisions:\\n- The union authenticators (both request and token level) try each authenticator in sequence until one succeeds\\n- NewFailOnError() versions of union authenticators stop on first error rather than trying all options\\n- Caching is applied to avoid repeated authentication work for tokens\\n- The anonymous authenticator uses NewFailOnError() to ensure no actual authentication method falls back to anonymous\\n- Request-level authenticators handle different protocol variations (HTTP, WebSocket)\\n- Token-level authenticators handle different token formats (CSV, JWT, bootstrap tokens, webhook)\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":8058,"cache_read_input_tokens":100822,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":8058},"output_tokens":6,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"2e960d17-1ee1-4234-a0f5-2a521a63cd98","uuid":"d2252fd2-6a76-46b1-8445-ecea5643d07e"}

a specific order. The main entry point is the Config.New() function in pkg/kubeapiserver/authenticator/config.go, which constructs the complete authentication chain.\\n\\nThe authentication chain has two levels:\\n\\n1. REQUEST AUTHENTICATORS - These process HTTP requests directly:\\n   - The request union authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/union/union.go) chains multiple request authenticators\\n   - Front-proxy/header-based authenticator (headerrequest) for front proxy scenarios\\n   - Client certificate (x509) authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/x509/x509.go) - verifies client certificates and extracts user info from CommonName and Organization\\n   - Bearer token authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/bearertoken/bearertoken.go) - extracts bearer tokens from Authorization header\\n   - WebSocket protocol authenticator for WebSocket upgrades\\n   - Anonymous authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/anonymous/anonymous.go) - allows unauthenticated access as system:anonymous user\\n\\n2. TOKEN AUTHENTICATORS - These verify extracted bearer tokens:\\n   - Token file authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/token/tokenfile/tokenfile.go) - verifies tokens from a CSV file\\n   - Service account JWT authenticator (pkg/serviceaccount/jwt.go) - verifies Kubernetes service account tokens using JWT validation\\n   - Bootstrap token authenticator (plugin/pkg/auth/authenticator/token/bootstrap/bootstrap.go) - handles cluster bootstrap tokens from kube-system namespace\\n   - Webhook token authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/authenticator/token/webhook/webhook.go) - delegates token verification to a webhook server\\n   - Token caching authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/token/cache/cache.go) - caches authentication results\\n\\nThe complete chain construction flow in Config.New() is:\\n1. Request authenticators are added first: front-proxy header authenticator, then client certificates\\n2. Token authenticators are combined into a union via tokenunion.New()\\n3. The token union is wrapped with caching if configured\\n4. Bearer token request authenticator wraps the token union to extract and verify bearer tokens\\n5. The request authenticators union (union.New()) combines all request authenticators\\n6. AuthenticatedGroupAdder wraps the chain to add system:authenticated group to successful authentications\\n7. Finally, the anonymous authenticator is added as a fallback using NewFailOnError() to handle unauthenticated requests\\n\\nThe delegating authenticator factory (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/authenticatorfactory/delegating.go) provides a similar but simpler chain for non-API-server components that need to verify tokens against the API server.\\n\\nKey architectural decisions:\\n- The union authenticators (both request and token level) try each authenticator in sequence until one succeeds\\n- NewFailOnError() versions of union authenticators stop on first error rather than trying all options\\n- Caching is applied to avoid repeated authentication work for tokens\\n- The anonymous authenticator uses NewFailOnError() to ensure no actual authentication method falls back to anonymous\\n- Request-level authenticators handle different protocol variations (HTTP, WebSocket)\\n- Token-level authenticators handle different token formats (CSV, JWT, bootstrap tokens, webhook)\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
